data-sentry-source-file="index.tsx"><div class="styles_htmlText__paMOf text-16 font-normal text-dark-gray styles_format__lYsGI styles_richText__JVzKB text-gray-600"><p>Hello Product Hunt 👋</p><br/><p>Today is a big day for us. We're excited to share Airial Travel with the Product Hunt community. Airial is the personal travel agent with AI superpowers. Simply describe your trip to Airial or drop in your favorite travel TikToks or IG reels and watch your dream trip come to life, fully planned and ready to book!</p><br/><p>Sanjeev <a href="https://www.producthunt.com/@sanjeev_shenoy1" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">@sanjeev_shenoy1</a> and I co-founded Airial Travel a year ago to solve a problem we faced repeatedly. Being avid travelers, we were traveling for several months a year and spending multiple days planning and booking each trip. Hours and hours of research, browsing, watching videos, form-filling, spreadsheets, refinements etc. As we dug deeper, we realized that the scale and the intensity of this problem is stunning - hundreds of millions of trips are booked online every year and planning each of them takes over five hours on average.</p><br/><p>Our vision <em>“Just imagine your trip, and Airial it!”</em> stems from our ultimate wish as travelers - AI that can figure out all the intricacies of trip planning for you - hotels, activities, flights, trains, transits, deals, date options, restaurants, interests, research, travel videos and everything else.</p><br/><p>Airial is the only travel planner out there today which creates plans crafted to the last detail, like a a travel agent truly would. We pick flights, hotels, transportation and plan every single day of your trip in detail around these choices and your preferences. The defining features that set us apart from competition originate from the core beliefs that Airial is built on:</p><ul><li><p>📅 <strong>Detailed intricately crafted plans:</strong> Attention to detail makes trip plans incredible. Airial plans trips in a level of detail that is simply unmatched, taking care of hundreds of common sense constraints across thousands of variables in seconds.</p></li><li><p>🚀 <strong>From Reels to Itineraries:</strong> TikTok / IG reels to Trips is work that millions do manually. We now enable all this in a click. This is the intersection of the two big trends in travel - AI and Socials.</p></li><li><p>🏖️ <strong>Personalized Planning:</strong> Travel portals today are one-size-fits-all. We plan trips tailored to your specific interests - architecture tours, scenic hikes or samurai sword fighting lessons!</p></li><li><p>👆 <strong>Actionable Itineraries:</strong> Just having a chatbot pick out one combination for you isn’t practically useful. Which was the last trip you planned that didn’t need any refinement? Every decision Airial makes for you is changeable via chat or UI controls.</p></li><li><p>🌎 <strong>Discovery in context:</strong> As you plan your trip, Airial gives you the tools to discover incredible ideas and expert advice specific to your itinerary and interests which can be instantly imported into your trip.</p></li></ul><br/><p>Vacations are for relaxation. Planning them shouldn’t be an added burden. With Airial, planning trips is as easy as dreaming them up!</p></div></div></div><div class="mt-2 flex justify-center"><button class="flex min-w-36 flex-row items-center justify-center gap-1
